   <script type="text/javascript">
    function search(all) {
     
     $(".productPreviewBox").css('opacity', 0.3); 
     if(all == 1) {
     setTimeout(loadsearch(1),800);
     } else {
     setTimeout(loadsearch(0),800);
     }
 
 }      
       
         
 function loadsearch(all) {
   text = document.getElementById("keyword").value;
   text = escape(text);
   
   
   var desc = $("#desc").is(':checked'); 
   var anzahl_erg = $('#anzahl-erg').val();
   var search_manu = $('#search_manu').val();
   var search_cat = $('#search_cat').val();
   
   
   var lang = getlang();
   
   laenge = document.getElementById('keyword').value.length;
 
   if(laenge > 2) {
          
      $("#keyword").addClass("load");
     
     if(all == 1) {
     var url = '?key='+text+'\u0026lang='+lang+'\u0026desc='+desc+'\u0026anzahl=0\u0026manu='+search_manu+'\u0026cat='+search_cat;
     } else {
     var url = '?key='+text+'\u0026lang='+lang+'\u0026desc='+desc+'\u0026anzahl='+anzahl_erg+'\u0026manu='+search_manu+'\u0026cat='+search_cat;
     }
     
 
     $("#content").load("search.php"+url, function() {
         $("#search2").fadeIn("slow"); 
         $("#keyword").removeClass("load");
         
         //setTimeout(window.location.hash=url,5000);
 	 setTimeout(history.pushState(null, "APM Suche", "http://www.apm-telescopes.de/index.html" + url),5000);
 
 
 
 //history.pushState(null, "APM Suche", "http://www.apm-telescopes.de/index.html" + url);
      
 
         
     });
     
 
     
   }
 
   if(laenge <= 2) {
     $("#search2").fadeOut("slow");
   }
 
 }
    
  
 function slideUp() {
   $("#search2").fadeOut("slow");
 }
 
 
 
 
 // 1200, 1050, 1024, 900, 768, 720 
 
     function background() {
       
       var x = screen.height;
       
       if(x <= 720) {
         $("body").addClass("background720");
       } else {
       
           if (x <= 1050)
           {
             $("body").addClass("background1050");
           } else {
               if (x <= 1200)
               {
                 $("body").addClass("background1200");
               }
           } 
       }  
     } 
   
   xx = document.URL.split("?key");
   //alert(xx[1]);
   
   var contentstring = "?key" + xx[1];
 var suchstring = /(key)/g;
  
 
 
 var suchergebnis = suchstring.test( document.URL);
 
 if (suchergebnis != false) {
     jQuery(document).ready(function() {  
       $("#content").load("search.php?key"+xx[1], function() {
         //$("#search2").slideDown("slow"); 
         //$("#keyword").removeClass("load");
         //window.location.hash=url;
         //alert('Das Suchwort ist im Text vorhanden!');
     });
      }); 
   
 }
   </script>

    function selectWert(sObj) {
     with (sObj) return x = options[selectedIndex].value;

 <script>
 
 
 
 function createRequestObject() {
     var ro;
     var browser = navigator.appName;
     if(browser == "Microsoft Internet Explorer"){
         ro = new ActiveXObject("Microsoft.XMLHTTP");
     }else{
         ro = new XMLHttpRequest();
     }
     return ro;
 }
 
 var http = createRequestObject();
 
 function handleResponse() 
 	{
     if(http.readyState == 4){
         var response = http.responseText;
         //document.getElementById('test1').innerHTML=response
     }
 	}
     
 function fader()
 {

     	http.send(null);
     
 		});

 }

   <script type="text/javascript">
    function search(all) {
     
     $(".productPreviewBox").css('opacity', 0.3); 
     if(all == 1) {
     setTimeout(loadsearch(1),800);
     } else {
     setTimeout(loadsearch(0),800);
     }
 
 }      
       
         
 function loadsearch(all) {
   text = document.getElementById("keyword").value;
   text = escape(text);
   
   
   var desc = $("#desc").is(':checked'); 
   var anzahl_erg = $('#anzahl-erg').val();
   var search_manu = $('#search_manu').val();
   var search_cat = $('#search_cat').val();
   
   
   var lang = getlang();
   
   laenge = document.getElementById('keyword').value.length;
 
   if(laenge > 2) {
          
      $("#keyword").addClass("load");
     
     if(all == 1) {
     var url = '?key='+text+'\u0026lang='+lang+'\u0026desc='+desc+'\u0026anzahl=0\u0026manu='+search_manu+'\u0026cat='+search_cat;
     } else {
     var url = '?key='+text+'\u0026lang='+lang+'\u0026desc='+desc+'\u0026anzahl='+anzahl_erg+'\u0026manu='+search_manu+'\u0026cat='+search_cat;
     }
     
 
     $("#content").load("search.php"+url, function() {
         $("#search2").fadeIn("slow"); 
         $("#keyword").removeClass("load");
         
         //setTimeout(window.location.hash=url,5000);
 	 setTimeout(history.pushState(null, "APM Suche", "http://www.apm-telescopes.de/index.html" + url),5000);

     $("#search2").fadeOut("slow");

   $("#search2").fadeOut("slow");
 }
 
 
 
 
 // 1200, 1050, 1024, 900, 768, 720 
 
     function background() {
       
       var x = screen.height;
       
       if(x <= 720) {
         $("body").addClass("background720");
       } else {
       
           if (x <= 1050)
           {
             $("body").addClass("background1050");
           } else {
               if (x <= 1200)
               {
                 $("body").addClass("background1200");
               }
           } 
       }  
     }

 <script>
 
 
 
 function createRequestObject() {
     var ro;
     var browser = navigator.appName;
     if(browser == "Microsoft Internet Explorer"){
         ro = new ActiveXObject("Microsoft.XMLHTTP");
     }else{
         ro = new XMLHttpRequest();
     }
     return ro;
 }
 
 var http = createRequestObject();
 
 function handleResponse() 
 	{
     if(http.readyState == 4){
         var response = http.responseText;
         //document.getElementById('test1').innerHTML=response
     }
 	}
     
 function fader()
 {
 	
 		jQuery( "#kcontent" ).fadeOut( "7000", function() {
 		// Animation complete
 		
 		document.getElementById("kcontent").innerHTML="<a href=\"javascript:kalenderhinweis()\"><img src=\"http://www.apm-telescopes.de/wi_daten/kalender/products/23_apm_slider_klein_de.jpg\"></A>";

 		// Animation complete
 		
 		http.open('GET', 'http://www.apm-telescopes.de/index.php?action=xmas');
     	http.onreadystatechange = handleResponse;
     	http.send(null);
     
 		});

 }

    function search(all) {
     
     $(".productPreviewBox").css('opacity', 0.3); 
     if(all == 1) {
     setTimeout(loadsearch(1),800);
     } else {
     setTimeout(loadsearch(0),800);
     }
 
 }      
       
         
 function loadsearch(all) {
   text = document.getElementById("keyword").value;
   text = escape(text);
   
   
   var desc = $("#desc").is(':checked'); 
   var anzahl_erg = $('#anzahl-erg').val();
   var search_manu = $('#search_manu').val();
   var search_cat = $('#search_cat').val();
   
   
   var lang = getlang();
   
   laenge = document.getElementById('keyword').value.length;
 
   if(laenge > 2) {
          
      $("#keyword").addClass("load");
     
     if(all == 1) {
     var url = '?key='+text+'\u0026lang='+lang+'\u0026desc='+desc+'\u0026anzahl=0\u0026manu='+search_manu+'\u0026cat='+search_cat;
     } else {
     var url = '?key='+text+'\u0026lang='+lang+'\u0026desc='+desc+'\u0026anzahl='+anzahl_erg+'\u0026manu='+search_manu+'\u0026cat='+search_cat;
     }
     
 
     $("#content").load("search.php"+url, function() {
         $("#search2").fadeIn("slow"); 
         $("#keyword").removeClass("load");
         
         //setTimeout(window.location.hash=url,5000);
 	 setTimeout(history.pushState(null, "APM Suche", "http://www.apm-telescopes.de/index.html" + url),5000);
 
 
 
 //history.pushState(null, "APM Suche", "http://www.apm-telescopes.de/index.html" + url);
      
 
         
     });
     
 
     
   }
 
   if(laenge <= 2) {
     $("#search2").fadeOut("slow");
   }
 
 }
    
  
 function slideUp() {
   $("#search2").fadeOut("slow");
 }

     function background() {
       
       var x = screen.height;
       
       if(x <= 720) {
         $("body").addClass("background720");
       } else {
       
           if (x <= 1050)
           {
             $("body").addClass("background1050");
           } else {
               if (x <= 1200)
               {
                 $("body").addClass("background1200");
               }
           } 
       }  
     }

 function createRequestObject() {
     var ro;
     var browser = navigator.appName;
     if(browser == "Microsoft Internet Explorer"){
         ro = new ActiveXObject("Microsoft.XMLHTTP");
     }else{
         ro = new XMLHttpRequest();
     }
     return ro;
 }
 
 var http = createRequestObject();
 
 function handleResponse() 
 	{
     if(http.readyState == 4){
         var response = http.responseText;
         //document.getElementById('test1').innerHTML=response
     }
 	}
     
 function fader()
 {
 	
 		jQuery( "#kcontent" ).fadeOut( "7000", function() {
 		// Animation complete
 		
 		document.getElementById("kcontent").innerHTML="<a href=\"javascript:kalenderhinweis()\"><img src=\"http://www.apm-telescopes.de/wi_daten/kalender/products/23_apm_slider_klein_de.jpg\"></A>";
 		jQuery( "#kcontent" ).fadeIn( "7000", function() {
 		// Animation complete
 		
 		http.open('GET', 'http://www.apm-telescopes.de/index.php?action=xmas');
     	http.onreadystatechange = handleResponse;
     	http.send(null);
     
 		});
 		});
 		
 }

    function search(all) {
     
     $(".productPreviewBox").css('opacity', 0.3); 
     if(all == 1) {
     setTimeout(loadsearch(1),800);
     } else {
     setTimeout(loadsearch(0),800);
     }
 
 }      
       
         
 function loadsearch(all) {
   text = document.getElementById("keyword").value;
   text = escape(text);
   
   
   var desc = $("#desc").is(':checked'); 
   var anzahl_erg = $('#anzahl-erg').val();
   var search_manu = $('#search_manu').val();
   var search_cat = $('#search_cat').val();
   
   
   var lang = getlang();
   
   laenge = document.getElementById('keyword').value.length;
 
   if(laenge > 2) {
          
      $("#keyword").addClass("load");
     
     if(all == 1) {
     var url = '?key='+text+'\u0026lang='+lang+'\u0026desc='+desc+'\u0026anzahl=0\u0026manu='+search_manu+'\u0026cat='+search_cat;
     } else {
     var url = '?key='+text+'\u0026lang='+lang+'\u0026desc='+desc+'\u0026anzahl='+anzahl_erg+'\u0026manu='+search_manu+'\u0026cat='+search_cat;
     }
     
 
     $("#content").load("search.php"+url, function() {
         $("#search2").fadeIn("slow"); 
         $("#keyword").removeClass("load");
         
         //setTimeout(window.location.hash=url,5000);
 	 setTimeout(history.pushState(null, "APM Suche", "http://www.apm-telescopes.de/index.html" + url),5000);
 
 
 
 //history.pushState(null, "APM Suche", "http://www.apm-telescopes.de/index.html" + url);
      
 
         
     });
     
 
     
   }
 
   if(laenge <= 2) {
     $("#search2").fadeOut("slow");
   }
 
 }
    
  
 function slideUp() {
   $("#search2").fadeOut("slow");
 }

     function background() {
       
       var x = screen.height;
       
       if(x <= 720) {
         $("body").addClass("background720");
       } else {
       
           if (x <= 1050)
           {
             $("body").addClass("background1050");
           } else {
               if (x <= 1200)
               {
                 $("body").addClass("background1200");
               }
           } 
       }  
     }

 <script>
 
 
 
 function createRequestObject() {
     var ro;
     var browser = navigator.appName;
     if(browser == "Microsoft Internet Explorer"){
         ro = new ActiveXObject("Microsoft.XMLHTTP");
     }else{
         ro = new XMLHttpRequest();
     }
     return ro;
 }
 
 var http = createRequestObject();
 
 function handleResponse() 
 	{
     if(http.readyState == 4){
         var response = http.responseText;
         //document.getElementById('test1').innerHTML=response
     }
 	}
     
 function fader()
 {
 	
 		jQuery( "#kcontent" ).fadeOut( "7000", function() {
 		// Animation complete
 		
 		document.getElementById("kcontent").innerHTML="<a href=\"javascript:kalenderhinweis()\"><img src=\"http://www.apm-telescopes.de/wi_daten/kalender/products/23_apm_slider_klein_de.jpg\"></A>";
 		jQuery( "#kcontent" ).fadeIn( "7000", function() {
 		// Animation complete
 		
 		http.open('GET', 'http://www.apm-telescopes.de/index.php?action=xmas');
     	http.onreadystatechange = handleResponse;
     	http.send(null);
     
 		});
 		});
 		
 }

    function search(all) {
     
     $(".productPreviewBox").css('opacity', 0.3); 
     if(all == 1) {
     setTimeout(loadsearch(1),800);
     } else {
     setTimeout(loadsearch(0),800);
     }
 
 }      
       
         
 function loadsearch(all) {
   text = document.getElementById("keyword").value;
   text = escape(text);
   
   
   var desc = $("#desc").is(':checked'); 
   var anzahl_erg = $('#anzahl-erg').val();
   var search_manu = $('#search_manu').val();
   var search_cat = $('#search_cat').val();
   
   
   var lang = getlang();
   
   laenge = document.getElementById('keyword').value.length;
 
   if(laenge > 2) {
          
      $("#keyword").addClass("load");
     
     if(all == 1) {
     var url = '?key='+text+'\u0026lang='+lang+'\u0026desc='+desc+'\u0026anzahl=0\u0026manu='+search_manu+'\u0026cat='+search_cat;
     } else {
     var url = '?key='+text+'\u0026lang='+lang+'\u0026desc='+desc+'\u0026anzahl='+anzahl_erg+'\u0026manu='+search_manu+'\u0026cat='+search_cat;
     }
     
 
     $("#content").load("search.php"+url, function() {
         $("#search2").fadeIn("slow"); 
         $("#keyword").removeClass("load");
         
         //setTimeout(window.location.hash=url,5000);
 	 setTimeout(history.pushState(null, "APM Suche", "http://www.apm-telescopes.de/index.html" + url),5000);
 
 
 
 //history.pushState(null, "APM Suche", "http://www.apm-telescopes.de/index.html" + url);
      
 
         
     });
     
 
     
   }
 
   if(laenge <= 2) {
     $("#search2").fadeOut("slow");
   }
 
 }
    
  
 function slideUp() {
   $("#search2").fadeOut("slow");
 }
 
 
 
 
 // 1200, 1050, 1024, 900, 768, 720 
 
     function background() {
       
       var x = screen.height;
       
       if(x <= 720) {
         $("body").addClass("background720");
       } else {
       
           if (x <= 1050)
           {
             $("body").addClass("background1050");
           } else {
               if (x <= 1200)
               {
                 $("body").addClass("background1200");
               }
           } 
       }  
     } 
   
   xx = document.URL.split("?key");
   //alert(xx[1]);
   
   var contentstring = "?key" + xx[1];
 var suchstring = /(key)/g;
  
 
 
 var suchergebnis = suchstring.test( document.URL);
 
 if (suchergebnis != false) {
     jQuery(document).ready(function() {

 <script>
 
 
 
 function createRequestObject() {
     var ro;
     var browser = navigator.appName;
     if(browser == "Microsoft Internet Explorer"){
         ro = new ActiveXObject("Microsoft.XMLHTTP");
     }else{
         ro = new XMLHttpRequest();
     }
     return ro;
 }
 
 var http = createRequestObject();
 
 function handleResponse() 
 	{
     if(http.readyState == 4){
         var response = http.responseText;
         //document.getElementById('test1').innerHTML=response
     }
 	}
     
 function fader()
 {
 	
 		jQuery( "#kcontent" ).fadeOut( "7000", function() {
 		// Animation complete
 		
 		document.getElementById("kcontent").innerHTML="<a href=\"javascript:kalenderhinweis()\"><img src=\"http://www.apm-telescopes.de/wi_daten/kalender/products/23_apm_slider_klein_de.jpg\"></A>";
 		jQuery( "#kcontent" ).fadeIn( "7000", function() {
 		// Animation complete
 		
 		http.open('GET', 'http://www.apm-telescopes.de/index.php?action=xmas');
     	http.onreadystatechange = handleResponse;
     	http.send(null);
     
 		});
 		});
 		
 }
